v_u_1.__index = v_u_1
v_u_1.__type = "Spring"
function v_u_1.__tostring(_)
	-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_1
	return v_u_1.__type
end
function v_u_1.new(p2, p3, p4, p5)
	-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_1
	local v6 = v_u_1
	local v7 = setmetatable({}, v6)
	v7.instant = false
	v7.marginOfError = 1e-6
	local v8 = p4 or 1
	local v9 = p3 * p3 / (4 * p2 * v8 * v8)
	v7.k = p2 / v9
	v7.d = -p3 / v9
	v7.x = p5
	v7.t = p5
	v7.v = p5 * 0
	return v7
end
function v_u_1.Update(p10, p11)
	if not p10.instant then
		local v12 = p10.t
		local v13 = p10.k
		local v14 = p10.d
		local v15 = p10.x
		local v16 = p10.v
		local v17 = v13 * (v12 - v15) + v16 * v14
		local v18 = v16 + v17 * (p11 / 2)
		local v19 = v13 * (v12 - (v15 + v16 * (p11 / 2))) + v18 * v14
		local v20 = v16 + v19 * (p11 / 2)
		local v21 = v13 * (v12 - (v15 + v18 * (p11 / 2))) + v20 * v14
		local v22 = v16 + v21 * p11
		local v23 = v15 + (v16 + 2 * (v18 + v20) + v22) * (p11 / 6)
		local v24 = v16 + (v17 + 2 * (v19 + v21) + v13 * (v12 - (v15 + v20 * p11)) + v22 * v14) * (p11 / 6)

		p10.v = v24
		local v25 = p10.t - v23
		local v26
		if type(v25) == "number" then
			v26 = math.abs(v25)
		else
			v26 = v25.Magnitude
		end
		if p10.marginOfError < v26 then
			return v23
		end
	end
	local v27 = p10.t
	local v28 = p10.v * 0
	p10.x = v27
	p10.v = v28

	["Name"] = "Number",
	["Default"] = "0",
	["Process"] = function(_, p1)
		local v2 = p1:gsub("[^%d.-]", "")
		local v3 = v2:sub(1, 1) .. v2:sub(2):gsub("%-", "")
		local v4 = v3:find("%.")
		if v4 then
			return v3:sub(1, v4) .. v3:sub(v4 + 1, #v3):gsub("[%.]", "")
		else

		end
	end,

			return false
		end

			return false
		end
		local v6 = p5:find("%.")
		return not v6 and true or not p5:sub(v6 + 1, #p5):find("%.")
	end,
	["ToType"] = function(p7, p8)
		local v9 = p7:Verify(p8) and p8 and p8 or p7.Default
		return tonumber(v9)
	end
}

	["Name"] = "Vector3",
	["Default"] = "0, 0, 0",
	["Process"] = function(_, p7)
		return p7
	end,

					if not v_u_1:Verify(v10) then
						return false
					end
				end
				return true
			end
		end
		return false
	end,
	["ToType"] = function(p11, p12)
		local v13 = p11:Verify(p12) and p12 and p12 or p11.Default
		local v14 = string.split(v13, ", ")
		for v15, v16 in next, v14 do

		end

		return Vector3.new(v17(v14))
	end

>>> SOURCE: StarterGui.GamepassGui.Gamepass Script
MPS = game:GetService("MarketplaceService")
local v1 = script.Parent
for _, v2 in pairs(v1:GetChildren()) do
	local v3 = v2.Name
	local v_u_4 = tonumber(v3)
	if v_u_4 then
		local v5 = MPS:GetProductInfo(v_u_4, Enum.InfoType.GamePass)
		if v5 then
			v2.Icon.Image = "http://www.roblox.com/asset/?id=" .. v5.IconImageAssetId
			v2.Description.Text = v5.Description
			v2.Price.Text = v5.PriceInRobux .. " R$"
			v2.BuyButton.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
				-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_4
				local v6 = game.Players.LocalPlayer
				MPS:PromptGamePassPurchase(v6, v_u_4)
			end)
		end
	end
end
<<< END SOURCE

MPS = game:GetService("MarketplaceService")
local v1 = script.Parent
for _, v2 in pairs(v1:GetChildren()) do
	local v3 = v2.Name
	local v_u_4 = tonumber(v3)
	if v_u_4 then
		local v5 = MPS:GetProductInfo(v_u_4, Enum.InfoType.GamePass)
		if v5 then
			v2.Icon.Image = "http://www.roblox.com/asset/?id=" .. v5.IconImageAssetId
			v2.Description.Text = v5.Description
			v2.Price.Text = v5.PriceInRobux .. " R$"
			v2.BuyButton.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
				-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_4
				local v6 = game.Players.LocalPlayer
				MPS:PromptGamePassPurchase(v6, v_u_4)
			end)
		end
	end
end

>>> SOURCE: StarterPlayer.StarterPlayerScripts.LocalScript
repeat
	wait()
until game.Players.LocalPlayer ~= nil
local v_u_1 = {}
local v_u_2 = {}
local v_u_3 = {}
local v_u_4 = {}
local v_u_5 = {}
local v6 = game:GetService("UserInputService")
local v_u_7 = game:GetService("RunService")
v_u_1.input = {}
v_u_1.mouse = game.Players.LocalPlayer:GetMouse()
function v_u_1.isClick(p8)
	return p8.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseButton1 and true or p8.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.Touch
end
v6.InputBegan:Connect(function(p9, p10)
	-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_1, (copy) v_u_3, (copy) v_u_7, (copy) v_u_2
	if not p10 then
		if v_u_1.isClick(p9) then
			v_u_1.input.Mouse1 = true
		end
		v_u_1.input\[p9.KeyCode.Value] \= true
		if p9.KeyCode \=\= Enum.KeyCode.Slash and not v_u_3.isDrawing then
			v_u_7.RenderStepped:Wait()
			v_u_2.chat.ChatBox:CaptureFocus()
		end
	end
end)
v6.InputEnded:Connect(function(p11, p12)
	-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_1
	if v_u_1.isClick(p11) then
		v_u_1.input.Mouse1 = false
	end
	if not p12 then
		v_u_1.input\[p11.KeyCode.Value] \= false
	end
end)
game:GetService("Debris")

function v_u_2.tweenifyButton(p_u_30, p31)
	-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_13
	local v_u_32 = p31 or 0.9
	local v_u_33 = Vector2.new(p_u_30.Size.X.Scale, p_u_30.Size.Y.Scale)
	local v_u_34 = Vector2.new(p_u_30.Size.X.Offset, p_u_30.Size.Y.Offset)
	p_u_30.MouseButton1Down:Connect(function()
		-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_13, (copy) p_u_30, (copy) v_u_33, (copy) v_u_32, (copy) v_u_34
		v_u_13:Create(p_u_30, TweenInfo.new(0.1), {
			["Size"] = UDim2.new(v_u_33.X * v_u_32, v_u_34.X * v_u_32, v_u_33.Y * v_u_32, v_u_34.Y * v_u_32)
		}):Play()
	end)
	p_u_30.MouseButton1Up:Connect(function()
		-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_13, (copy) p_u_30, (copy) v_u_33, (copy) v_u_34
		v_u_13:Create(p_u_30, TweenInfo.new(0.1), {
			["Size"] = UDim2.new(v_u_33.X, v_u_34.X, v_u_33.Y, v_u_34.Y)
		}):Play()
	end)
	p_u_30.MouseLeave:Connect(function()
		-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_13, (copy) p_u_30, (copy) v_u_33, (copy) v_u_34
		v_u_13:Create(p_u_30, TweenInfo.new(0.1), {
			["Size"] = UDim2.new(v_u_33.X, v_u_34.X, v_u_33.Y, v_u_34.Y)
		}):Play()
	end)
end

	-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_21, (copy) v_u_2

		["Position"] = UDim2.new(0.5, 0, 0.1, 0),

	}):Play()

		["Size"] = UDim2.fromScale(1, 1)

	}):Play()

	-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_21, (copy) v_u_2

function v_u_2.gameChoosingTween()
	-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_2, (copy) v_u_21

function v_u_2.theWord(p38)
	-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_2, (copy) v_u_20, (copy) v_u_3
	if p38 then

			if v_u_20.RobloxLocaleId == "en-us" then
				local v39 = ""
				if v_u_3.isDrawing then
					for v40 = 1, string.len(p38) do
						local v41 = string.sub(p38, v40, v40)
						if v41 == "_" then
							local v42 = v_u_2.word.Frame.word.Text
							v39 = v39 .. ("<font transparency=\"1.0\">%*</font>"):format((string.sub(v42, v40, v40)))
						else
							v39 = v39 .. v41
						end
					end
				end
				v_u_2.word.Frame.wordTint.Text = v39
			end
			if not v_u_3.hasGuessed then
				v_u_2.word.Backframe.HintButton.Visible = true
			end
		else
			v_u_2.word.Backframe.HintButton.Visible = false
		end
		v_u_2.word.Frame.word.Text = p38
	end
end

function v_u_18.OnBubbleAdded(p152, _)
	if p152.Text == "!guess" then
		p152.Text = "Guessed the word!"

local v_u_154 = v_u_18:WaitForChild("TextChannels")
v_u_18.MessageReceived:Connect(function(p155)
	-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_22, (copy) v_u_2, (copy) v_u_2
	local v156 = p155.TextSource
	if v156 then
		v156 = v_u_22:GetPlayerByUserId(v156.UserId)
	end
	if v156 then
		local v157 = p155.Text
		if p155.Status == Enum.TextChatMessageStatus.Floodchecked then
			print(p155.Metadata)
			print(p155.PrefixText)
			v_u_2.addChat("@", "Chat cooldown")
			return
		elseif p155.Status == Enum.TextChatMessageStatus.MessageTooLong then
			v_u_2.addChat("@", "Message too long")
			return
		elseif p155.Status == Enum.TextChatMessageStatus.ModerationTimeout then
			v_u_2.addChat("@", "Chat timeout")
		elseif string.len(v157) > 0 then
			v_u_2.addChat(v156, v157)
		end
	else
		return
	end
end)

	end
end)
local v_u_162 = 0
function v_u_2.warn(p163, p164)
	-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_162, (copy) v_u_2
	v_u_162 = v_u_162 + 1
	local v_u_165 = v_u_162
	v_u_2.warnPlayer.Enabled = true
	v_u_2.warnPlayer.Frame.Reason.Text = p163
	local v166 = string.format
	local v167 = p164 / 86400
	local v168 = math.floor(v167)
	local v169 = p164 / 3600
	local v170 = math.floor(v169) % 24

local function v_u_201(p184, p185)
	local v186 = p184.CFrame:PointToObjectSpace(p185)
	local v187 = p184.Size / 2
	local v188 = p184.CFrame
	local v189 = v186.X
	local v190 = -v187.X
	local v191 = v187.X
	local v192 = math.clamp(v189, v190, v191)
	local v193 = v186.Y
	local v194 = -v187.Y
	local v195 = v187.Y
	local v196 = math.clamp(v193, v194, v195)
	local v197 = v186.Z
	local v198 = -v187.Z
	local v199 = v187.Z
	local v200 = math.clamp(v197, v198, v199)
	return v188 * Vector3.new(v192, v196, v200)
end

function v_u_3.canUndo()
	-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_3
	return v_u_3.strokes[v_u_3.currentWaypoint]
end
function v_u_3.canRedo()
	-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_3
	return v_u_3.strokes[v_u_3.currentWaypoint + 1]
end
function v_u_3.setCurrentWaypoint(p283)
	-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_3, (copy) v_u_2
	local v284 = v_u_3
	local v285 = #v_u_3.strokes + 1
	v284.currentWaypoint = math.clamp(p283, 0, v285)
	v_u_2.drawTools.UndoRedo.Undo.BackgroundTransparency = v_u_3.canUndo() and 0 or 0.5
	v_u_2.drawTools.UndoRedo.Redo.BackgroundTransparency = v_u_3.canRedo() and 0 or 0.5
end
v_u_3.setCurrentWaypoint(0)
function v_u_3.setWaypoint(p286)
	-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_3, (copy) v_u_173, (copy) v_u_5
	v_u_3.setCurrentWaypoint(v_u_3.currentWaypoint + 1)
	for v287 = v_u_3.currentWaypoint, #v_u_3.strokes do
		v_u_3.strokes[v287] = nil
	end
	v_u_173.tempPixels:ClearAllChildren()
	v_u_3.strokes[v_u_3.currentWaypoint] = {}
	for v288 = 1, #v_u_3.lastStroke do
		v_u_3.strokes[v_u_3.currentWaypoint][v288] = v_u_3.lastStroke[v288]
	end
	v_u_3.lastStroke = {}
	if p286 then
		v_u_5.wayPoint:FireServer()
	end
	v_u_3.setCurrentWaypoint(v_u_3.currentWaypoint)
end
function v_u_3.addStroke(p289, p290)
	-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_3
	local v291 = v_u_3.lastStroke
	table.insert(v291, { p289, p290 })
end
function v_u_3.undo(p292)
	-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_3, (copy) v_u_173, (copy) v_u_5
	if v_u_3.canUndo() then
		for v293 = 1, #v_u_3.strokes[v_u_3.currentWaypoint] do
			local v294 = v_u_3.strokes[v_u_3.currentWaypoint]\[v293]
			if v294\[1].Parent then
				if v294\[2] then
					v294\[1].Parent \= v294\[1].Parent \=\= workspace.canvasPixels and v_u_173.erasedPixels or workspace.canvasPixels
				else
					v294\[1].Parent \= v294\[1].Parent \=\= workspace.canvasPixels and v_u_173.tempPixels or workspace.canvasPixels
				end
			end
		end
		v_u_3.setCurrentWaypoint(v_u_3.currentWaypoint - 1)
		if p292 then
			v_u_5.undoRedo:FireServer()
		end
	end
end
function v_u_3.redo(p295)
	-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_3, (copy) v_u_173, (copy) v_u_5
	if v_u_3.canRedo() then
		v_u_3.setCurrentWaypoint(v_u_3.currentWaypoint + 1)
		for v296 = 1, #v_u_3.strokes[v_u_3.currentWaypoint] do
			local v297 = v_u_3.strokes[v_u_3.currentWaypoint]\[v296]
			if v297\[1].Parent then
				if v297\[2] then
					v297\[1].Parent \= v297\[1].Parent \=\= workspace.canvasPixels and v_u_173.erasedPixels or workspace.canvasPixels
				else
					v297\[1].Parent \= v297\[1].Parent \=\= workspace.canvasPixels and v_u_173.tempPixels or workspace.canvasPixels
				end
			end
		end
		if p295 then
			v_u_5.undoRedo:FireServer(true)
		end
	end
end

function v_u_3.setCurrentColor(p298)
	-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_3, (copy) v_u_2
	local v299 = v_u_3
	local v300, v301, v302 = p298:ToHSV()
	local v303 = Color3.fromHSV
	local v304 = v301 * 1.1
	v299.currentColor = v303(v300, math.min(1, v304), v302 * 0.9)

function v_u_3.isColorEqual(p305, p306)
	local v307 = p305.R - p306.R
	local v308 = math.abs(v307)
	local v309 = p305.G - p306.G
	local v310 = v308 + math.abs(v309)
	local v311 = p305.B - p306.B
	return v310 + math.abs(v311) < 0.05
end
function v_u_3.addRecentColor(p312)
	-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_2, (copy) v_u_3, (copy) v_u_5, (ref) v_u_258, (copy) v_u_256
	local v313 = v_u_2.drawToolsFrames.Custom.Colors.RecentColors
	for v314 = 1, 10 do
		local v315 = v314 - 1
		local v316 = v313:FindFirstChild((tostring(v315)))
		if v_u_3.isColorEqual(p312, v316.BackgroundColor3) then
			v_u_3.setCurrentColor(v316.BackgroundColor3)
			v_u_5.drawTools:FireServer(v_u_3.pixelSize, v_u_3.currentColor)
			v_u_258 = v316
			v_u_256.Parent = v316
			v_u_256.Visible = true
			return
		end
	end
	for v317 = 10, 2, -1 do
		local v318 = v317 - 1
		local v319 = v313:FindFirstChild((tostring(v318)))
		local v320 = v317 - 2
		v319.BackgroundColor3 = v313:FindFirstChild((tostring(v320))).BackgroundColor3
	end
	local v321 = v313:FindFirstChild("0")
	v321.BackgroundColor3 = p312
	v_u_3.setCurrentColor(v321.BackgroundColor3)
	v_u_5.drawTools:FireServer(v_u_3.pixelSize, v_u_3.currentColor)
	v_u_258 = v321
	v_u_256.Parent = v321
	v_u_256.Visible = true
end

	-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_3
	if not p323 then
		local v324 = v_u_3.pixelLayer / 0.1
		p323 = math.floor(v324) + 1

end

function v_u_3.beginDraw()
	-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_3, (ref) v_u_281, (copy) v_u_280, (copy) v_u_176, (copy) v_u_177, (ref) v_u_336, (copy) v_u_1, (ref) v_u_337, (copy) v_u_2, (copy) v_u_201, (ref) v_u_335, (copy) v_u_231
	if v_u_3.isDrawing then
		v_u_3.updateLayer()
		if v_u_281 then
			v_u_280(v_u_176:GetMouseLocation() - Vector2.new(0, v_u_177.TopbarInset.Height))
			return
		elseif v_u_336 and v_u_1.mouse.Target.Name ~= "canvas" or v_u_337 then
			v_u_3.setContinueType("blank")
		else
			v_u_3.setContinueType("canvas")
			if v_u_2.drawToolsFrames.Custom.Visible then
				v_u_3.addRecentColor(v_u_3.getTrueCurrentColor())
			end
			local v338 = v_u_201(v_u_3.canvas, v_u_1.mouse.Hit.Position)
			if v_u_3.toolType == "pen" then
				if v_u_335 and (Vector2.new(v_u_335.Position.X, v_u_335.Position.Y) - Vector2.new(v338.X, v338.Y)).Magnitude < 0.1 then
					return
				end
				local v339 = v_u_3.drawPixel(v338.X, v338.Y)
				v_u_3.drawLine(v339, v_u_335 or v339)
				v_u_335 = v339
			elseif v_u_3.toolType == "eraser" then
				v_u_231.Transparency = 0
				v_u_3.erase(v338, true)
			end
			v_u_336 = false
		end
	else
		return
	end
end
function v_u_3.endDraw()
	-- upvalues: (copy) v_u_3, (ref) v_u_322, (ref) v_u_335, (ref) v_u_336, (ref) v_u_337, (ref) v_u_281, (copy) v_u_231

		end

		v_u_336 = true
		v_u_337 = false
		v_u_281 = false
		v_u_231.Transparency = 1
		v_u_3.setContinueType("")
	end
end
